		}
		
		if(isequipped(3001))
		{ 	bonus bAllStats,5;
			bonus bFleeRate,5;
			bonus bCriticalRate,5;
			bonus bDex,10;
			bonus bVit,10;
			if(getequiprefinerycnt(EQI_HEAD_LOW) == 10) { bonus bAllStats,15; bonus bFleeRate,10; }
		}
		
		if(isequipped(3002))
		{ 	bonus bAllStats,5;
			bonus bSpeedRate,25;
			bonus bAtkRate,5;
			bonus bCriticalRate,5;

		}
}

function	script	endow_r	{

		if(endowrand==0) { return; }
		if(endowrand==1) { sc_start SC_FIREWEAPON,600000,0; }
		if(endowrand==2) { sc_start SC_WATERWEAPON,600000,0; }
		if(endowrand==3) { sc_start SC_WINDWEAPON,600000,0; }

	return;
}

pay_arche,43,122,5	script	Endowmixer	754,{

	mes "[^0000ffEndowmixer^000000]";
	mes "Hello pick the endow you want for your SETs";
	menu "^0000ff>^000000 Fire",L_fire,
	"^0000ff>^000000 Water",L_water,
	"^0000ff>^000000 Wind",L_wind,
	"^0000ff>^000000 None",L_none;

L_fire:
	set endowrand,1;
	next;
	mes "[^0000ffEndowmixer^000000]";
	mes "Your Set will be endowed with ^ff0000Fire^000000 Property.";
	close;
	
L_water:
	set endowrand,2;
	next;
	mes "[^0000ffEndowmixer^000000]";
	mes "Your Set will be endowed with ^0000ffWater^000000 Property.";
	close;
L_wind:
	set endowrand,3;
	next;
	mes "[^0000ffEndowmixer^000000]";
	mes "Your Set will be endowed with ^ff8800Wind^000000 Property.";
	close;
L_none:
	set endowrand,0;
	next;
	mes "[^0000ffEndowmixer^000000]";
	mes "Your Set will be endowed with ^777777None^000000.";
	close;
}

//TransOrb

function	script	thirdclasselite	{
	if(BaseLevel < 255) goto L_notSup;
	goto L_choosejob;
	close;

//Choose Job
	L_choosejob:
	mes "^ff0000[Job Master]^000000";
	mes "Welcome, please select the job you wish to change into";
	menu "RuneKnight",L_RuneKnight, "ArchBishop", L_ArchBishop, "Warlock", L_Warlock, "Mechanic", L_Mechanic, "Ranger", L_Ranger, "GuillotineCross", L_GuillotineCross, "RoyalGuard",  L_RoyalGuard, "Sura", L_Sura, "Sorcerer", L_Sorcerer, "ShadowChaser", L_ShadowChaser, "Genetic", L_Genetic, "Minstrel", L_Minstrel, "Wanderer", L_Wanderer, "Nevermind", L_quit;
	close;

// Change to Rune Knight
	L_RuneKnight:
		mes "^ff0000[Job Master]^000000";
		mes "Do you want to change into a Rune Knight?";
		menu "No",L_quit,"Yes",-;
			jobchange 4060;
			ResetSkill;
			set SkillPoint,158;
			close;
// Change to Arch Bishop
	L_ArchBishop:
		mes "^ff0000[Job Master]^000000";
		mes "Do you want to change into an Arch Bishop?";
		menu "No",L_quit,"Yes",-;
			jobchange 4063;
			ResetSkill;
			set SkillPoint,158;
			close;	
// Change to Warlock
	L_Warlock:
		mes "^ff0000[Job Master]^000000";
		mes "Do you want to change into a Warlock?";
		menu "No",L_quit,"Yes",-;
			jobchange 4061;
			ResetSkill;
			set SkillPoint,158;
			close;	
// Change to Mechanic			
	L_Mechanic:
		mes "^ff0000[Job Master]^000000";
		mes "Do you want to change into a Mechanic?";
		menu "No",L_quit,"Yes",-;
			jobchange 4064;
			ResetSkill;
			set SkillPoint,158;
			close;	
// Change to Ranger			
	L_Ranger:

		mes "Do you want to change into a Ranger?";
		menu "No",L_quit,"Yes",-;
			jobchange 4062;
			ResetSkill;
			set SkillPoint,158;

			ResetSkill;
			set SkillPoint,158;
			jobchange 4073;
			close;	
// Change to Sura

		mes "Do you want to change into a Sura?";
		menu "No",L_quit,"Yes",-;
			ResetSkill;
			set SkillPoint,158;
			jobchange 4077;
			close;	
// Change Sorcerer			
	L_Sorcerer:

		mes "I'm sorry, you do not seem to have enough Base Levels";
		mes "Please come again soon!";
		close;
